add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Removing temporary ideas
	id = annex.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.0"}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		remove_ideas = NoDoubleAnnexItalyEvent
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Flanders-Wallonia
	id = annex.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.1"}
	title = annex.1.t
	desc = annex.1.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.1.a
		add_political_power = 60
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = BEL }
			annex_country = {
				target = BEL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = WLL }
			annex_country = {
				target = WLL
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_war_with = FLN }
			annex_country = {
				target = FLN
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Swiss liberation
	id = annex.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.2"}
	title = annex.2.t
	desc = annex.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}

		SWI = {
			add_state_core = 760
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			SWI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = FRA
					tag = NFA
					tag = FRP
					tag = OCC
					owns_state = 16
					owns_state = 21
				}
				owns_state = 943
			}
			SWI = {
				transfer_state = 943
			}
		}

		SWI = {
			clr_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			clr_country_flag = SWI_enemies_on_all_sides
			clr_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			clr_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance

			set_cosmetic_tag = SWI
		}

		puppet = SWI

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = FRA
			}
			SWI = {
				set_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #Take Romandie
		name = annex.2.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		trigger = {
			tag = FRA
			owns_state = 760
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					state = 760
				}
			}

			SWI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		SWI = {
			clr_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
			clr_country_flag = SWI_enemies_on_all_sides
			clr_country_flag = SWI_GER_alliance
			clr_country_flag = SWI_AUS_alliance

			set_cosmetic_tag = SWI
		}

		puppet = SWI

		SWI = {
			set_country_flag = SWI_bend_france
		}

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = SWITZ_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Bulgaria
	id = annex.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.3"}
	title = annex.3.t
	desc = annex.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
			}
			add_state_claim = 841
			add_state_claim = 106
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GRE
			}
			add_state_core = 731
			add_state_claim = 769
			add_state_claim = 184
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ROM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RRM
			}
			add_state_claim = 77
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUL
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			BUL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BUL

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

					add_state_core = 80

			}

			}

			every_owned_state = {

						is_core_of = ROM

						is_core_of = ROOT

		}

		if = {
			limit = {

	option = { #Take Bessarabia
		name = annex.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}

				has_government = national_populist

				remove_state_core = 78

				remove_state_core = 78
			}

						is_core_of = ROM
						is_core_of = RRM
					}

			}

country_event = { #Serbian liberation
	id = annex.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.8"}
	title = annex.8.t
	desc = annex.8.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					state = 108
					state = 765
					state = 767
					state = 107
				}
				is_core_of = SER
			}
			SER = { remove_state_core = PREV }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 841
				NOT = { 841 = { is_core_of = SER } }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 48
						841 = { is_core_of = BUL }
					}
				}
			}
			SER = { add_state_core = 841 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 106
				NOT = { 106 = { is_core_of = SER } }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						owns_state = 48
						106 = { is_core_of = BUL }
					}
				}
			}
			SER = { add_state_core = 106 }
		}


		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SER
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			SER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = SER

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #greek liberation
	id = annex.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.10"}
	title = annex.10.t
	desc = annex.10.d

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.10.b #Liberate Greece as republic
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = AUS
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = GBR
					AND = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						is_in_europe = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			not_has_socialist_government = yes
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GRE
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			GRE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		GRE = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				GRE_stop_being_syndicalist = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom }
				GRE_restore_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum }
				clr_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
				set_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
			}
		}
		puppet = GRE
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.10.c #Liberate Kingdom of Greece
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					tag = GER
					tag = AUS
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = GBR
					AND = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						is_in_europe = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			not_has_socialist_government = yes
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GRE
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			GRE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		GRE = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				GRE_stop_being_syndicalist = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GRE_memories_of_king }
				remove_ideas = GRE_memories_of_king
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_king_alexandros }
					hidden_effect = { country_event = gre.25 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_king_georgios }
					hidden_effect = { country_event = gre.26 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_restore_monarchy }
					hidden_effect = { country_event = gre.27 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_monarchy_referendum }
						ROOT = { has_elected_government = yes }
					}
					set_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = GRE_monarchy_referendum
						has_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
					}
					set_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
					clr_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { has_dictatorship_government = yes } }
					hidden_effect = { country_event = gre.27 }
				}
				else = {
					hidden_effect = { country_event = gre.25 }
				}
			}
		}
		puppet = GRE
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.10.e #Liberate Hellenic Commune
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GRE
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			GRE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		GRE = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom }
				GRE_restore_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_socialist_government = yes } }

				set_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
			}
		}
		puppet = GRE
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = GRE_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GUA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			GUA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = GUA

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
					AND = {
						tag = NIC
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			GUA = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = radical_socialist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							tag = NIC
						}
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			GUA = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
			GUA = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.64.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = GUA_CONQ
		add_political_power = -60
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_war_support = -0.03
	}

				}
			}
			FRP = {

		}
	}

		}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Persia

	id = annex.109
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.109"}
	title = annex.109.t
	desc = annex.109.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = OTT
				}
				add_state_claim = 413
				add_state_claim = 421
				add_state_claim = 417
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.109.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05

		set_country_flag = PER_CONQ

	}

	option = { #puppet

		name = annex.109.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = PER
					AND = {
						state = 352
						ROOT = {
							NOT = { owns_state = 291 }
							NOT = { owns_state = 49 }
						}
					}
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					region = 28
					region = 129
				}
			}

			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = PER

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					not_has_socialist_government = yes
				}
				PER = {
					remove_ideas = PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
					remove_ideas = PER_evolution_idea
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							not_has_elected_government = yes
						}
						PER = {
							remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									not_has_authoritarian_government = yes
								}
								PER = {
									remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = PER_REP }
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #iran and kurdistan

		name = annex.109.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = OTT }
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = KUR
				KUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { country_exists = KUR }
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = KUR
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			KUR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = KUR
					KUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
			puppet = KUR
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = PER
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					region = 28
					region = 129
				}
			}

			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = PER

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					not_has_socialist_government = yes
				}
				PER = {
					remove_ideas = PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
					remove_ideas = PER_evolution_idea
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							not_has_elected_government = yes
						}
						PER = {
							remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
						}
						else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									not_has_authoritarian_government = yes
								}
								PER = {
									remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = PER_REP }
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
		}

	}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Siam

	id = annex.118
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.118"}
	title = annex.118.t
	desc = annex.118.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet - Mahidol
		name = annex.118.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = GEX
				tag = RUS
				tag = UKR
			}
		}

		### Khmer Krom
		# Saigon - 286 (VIE > CAM > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = VIE
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 287 # Annam
					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
				}
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
			VIE = { transfer_state = 286 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 286 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 286 # Saigon
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 286 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 286 }
		}
		# Mekong Delta - 856 (VIE > CAM > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = VIE
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 287 # Annam
					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 286 # Saigon
				}
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			VIE = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}

		### Cambodia
		# Phra Tabong - 825 (SIA > CAM > INC; available if tag's Cambodia or Indochinese)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
				}
				owns_state = 825 # Phra Tabong
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 825 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 825 # Phra Tabong
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 825 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 825 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 825 # Phra Tabong
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 825 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 825 }
		}
		# Phnom Penh - 750 (CAM > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
				}
				owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 750 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 750 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 750 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 750 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 750 }
		}
		# Stung Treng - 826 (CAM > VIE > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAM
					tag = VIE
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 287 # Annam
					owns_state = 670 # Laos
					owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
					owns_state = 286 # Saigon
					owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
				}
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 826 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
			VIE = { transfer_state = 826 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 826 }
		}

		### Laos
		# Laos - 670 (LAO > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = LAO
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 827 # Annam
					owns_state = 671 # Hanoi
				}
				owns_state = 670 # Laos
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 670 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LAO = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 670 # Laos
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 670 }
			LAO = { transfer_state = 670 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 670 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 670 }
		}
		# Chaiyaburi - 882 (SIA > LAO > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = LAO
					tag = INC
				}
				owns_state = 882 # Chaiyaburi
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 882 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LAO = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 882 # Chaiyaburi
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 882 }
			LAO = { transfer_state = 882 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 882 # Chaiyaburi
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 882 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 882 }
		}

		### Malaya
		# Singapur - 336 (Assuming Direct Control)
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 336 # Singapur
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 336 }
		}
		# Sirat Malai - 751 (SIA > MLY)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MLY
					owns_state = 846 # Malaya
				}
				owns_state = 751 # Sirat Malai
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 751 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MLY = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 751 # Sirat Malai
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 751 }
			MLY = { transfer_state = 751 }
		}
		# Malaya - 846 (MLY)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MLY
					owns_state = 336 # Singapur
				}
				owns_state = 846 # Malaya
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 846 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MLY = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 846 # Malaya
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 846 }
			MLY = { transfer_state = 846 }
		}
		# Pattani - 830 (SIA >> MLY; only available if Malaya is out there)
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = MLY
				owns_state = 830 # Pattani
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 830 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MLY = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 830 # Pattani
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 830 }
			MLY = { transfer_state = 830 }
		}

		### Burma
		# Upper Shan - 72 (SHA > BUR)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SHA
					tag = BUR
					owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				}
				owns_state = 72 # Upper Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 72 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 72 # Upper Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 72 }
			SHA = { transfer_state = 72 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 72 # Upper Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 72 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 72 }
		}
		# Lower Shan - 756 (SHA > BUR)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SHA
					tag = BUR
					owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				}
				owns_state = 756 # Lower Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 756 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 756 # Lower Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 756 }
			SHA = { transfer_state = 756 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 756 # Lower Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 756 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 756 }
		}
		# Morlamaeng - 831 (BUR)
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUR
				owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				owns_state = 831 # Morlamaeng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 831 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 831 # Morlamaeng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 831 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 831 }
		}
		# Tanaosri - 749 (SIA > BUR; Only available if Burma is around)
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUR
				owns_state = 749 # Tanaosri
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 749 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 749 # Tanaosri
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 749 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 749 }
		}

		### Other Remaining parts becaming Siamese puppet

					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 286 # Saigon
				}
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			VIE = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 856 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 856 }
		}

		### Cambodia
		# Phra Tabong - 825 (SIA > CAM > INC; available if tag's Cambodia or Indochinese)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
				}
				owns_state = 825 # Phra Tabong
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 825 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 825 # Phra Tabong
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 825 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 825 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 825 # Phra Tabong
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 825 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 825 }
		}
		# Phnom Penh - 750 (CAM > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
				}
				owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 750 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 750 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 750 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 750 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 750 }
		}
		# Stung Treng - 826 (CAM > VIE > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = CAM
					tag = VIE
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 287 # Annam
					owns_state = 670 # Laos
					owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
					owns_state = 286 # Saigon
					owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
				}
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
			CAM = { transfer_state = 826 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIE = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
			VIE = { transfer_state = 826 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 826 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 826 }
		}

		### Laos
		# Laos - 670 (LAO > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = LAO
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 827 # Annam
					owns_state = 671 # Hanoi
				}
				owns_state = 670 # Laos
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 670 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LAO = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 670 # Laos
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 670 }
			LAO = { transfer_state = 670 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 670 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 670 }
		}
		# Chaiyaburi - 882 (SIA > LAO > INC)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = LAO
					tag = INC
				}
				owns_state = 882 # Chaiyaburi
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 882 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LAO = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 882 # Chaiyaburi
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 882 }
			LAO = { transfer_state = 882 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				INC = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 882 # Chaiyaburi
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 882 }
			INC = { transfer_state = 882 }
		}

		### Malaya
		# Singapur - 336 (Assuming Direct Control)
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 336 # Singapur
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 336 }
		}
		# Sirat Malai - 751 (SIA > MLY)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MLY
					owns_state = 846 # Malaya
				}
				owns_state = 751 # Sirat Malai
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 751 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MLY = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 751 # Sirat Malai
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 751 }
			MLY = { transfer_state = 751 }
		}
		# Malaya - 846 (MLY)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MLY
					owns_state = 336 # Singapur
				}
				owns_state = 846 # Malaya
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 846 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MLY = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 846 # Malaya
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 846 }
			MLY = { transfer_state = 846 }
		}
		# Pattani - 830 (SIA >> MLY; only available if Malaya is out there)
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = MLY
				owns_state = 830 # Pattani
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 830 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MLY = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 830 # Pattani
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 830 }
			MLY = { transfer_state = 830 }
		}

		### Burma
		# Upper Shan - 72 (SHA > BUR)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SHA
					tag = BUR
					owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				}
				owns_state = 72 # Upper Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 72 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 72 # Upper Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 72 }
			SHA = { transfer_state = 72 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 72 # Upper Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 72 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 72 }
		}
		# Lower Shan - 756 (SHA > BUR)
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = SHA
					tag = BUR
					owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				}
				owns_state = 756 # Lower Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 756 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 756 # Lower Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 756 }
			SHA = { transfer_state = 756 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 756 # Lower Shan
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 756 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 756 }
		}
		# Morlamaeng - 831 ( BUR )
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUR
				owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				owns_state = 831 # Morlamaeng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 831 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 831 # Morlamaeng
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 831 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 831 }
		}
		# Tanaosri - 749 (SIA > BUR; Only available if Burma is around)
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUR
				owns_state = 749 # Tanaosri
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 749 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				owns_state = 749 # Tanaosri
			}
			SIA = { remove_state_core = 749 }
			BUR = { transfer_state = 749 }
		}

		### Other Remaining parts becaming Siamese puppet
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SIA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
			}
			SIA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		# Emergency transfer as these area tended to lack cores
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = SHA
					tag = BUR
					owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				}
				owns_state = 72 # Upper Shan
			}
			SIA = { transfer_state = 72 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = SHA
					tag = BUR
					owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				}
				owns_state = 756 # Lower Shan
			}
			SIA = { transfer_state = 756 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = BUR
					owns_state = 288 # Yangon
				}
				owns_state = 831 # Morlamaeng
			}
			SIA = { transfer_state = 831 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = CAM
					tag = INC
					owns_state = 826 # Stung Treng
					owns_state = 856 # Mekong Delta
				}
				owns_state = 750 # Phnom Penh
			}
			SIA = { transfer_state = 750 }
		}
		puppet = SIA

		if = {
			limit = { SIA = { NOT = { has_global_flag = SIA_THAILAND } } }
			SIA = { set_cosmetic_tag = SIA_REP }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SIA = { has_cosmetic_tag = THI } }
			SIA = { set_cosmetic_tag = THI_REP }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			SIA = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = SIA_SIAM }
					set_cosmetic_tag = SIA_REP
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_global_flag = SIA_THAILAND
							has_cosmetic_tag = THI
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = THI_REP
					set_party_name = { # CPT
						ideology = totalist
						long_name = SIA_totalist_party_TH_long
						name = SIA_totalist_party_TH
					}
					set_party_name = { # KST
						ideology = syndicalist
						long_name = SIA_syndicalist_party_TH_long
						name = SIA_syndicalist_party_TH
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = SIA_SIAM
							has_global_flag = SIA_THAILAND
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = SIA_REP
				}
				set_party_name = { # Chart Sangkhom Party
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = SIA_paternal_autocrat_party_sarit_long
					name = SIA_paternal_autocrat_party_sarit
				}
				create_country_leader = { # Republican Totalism - Song Noppakul
					name = "Song Noppakul"
					desc = "POLITICS_SONG_NOPPAKUL_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/SIA/Portrait_Siam_Song_Noppakul.tga"
					expire = "2012.11.27"
					ideology = totalist_subtype
					traits = { permanent_revolutionary }
				}
				create_country_leader = { # Pridi Panomyong
					name = "Pridi Phanomyong"
					desc = "POLITICS_PRIDI_PANOMYONG_REBEL_WIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/SIA/Portrait_Siam_Pridi_Panomyong_II.tga"
					expire = "1983.5.2"
					ideology = syndicalist_subtype
					traits = { }
				}
				create_country_leader = { # Pridi Panomyong
					name = "Pridi Phanomyong"
					desc = "POLITICS_PRIDI_PANOMYONG_REBEL_WIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/SIA/Portrait_Siam_Pridi_Panomyong_II.tga"
					expire = "1983.5.2"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = { }
				}
				create_country_leader = { # Pridi Panomyong
					name = "Pridi Phanomyong"
					desc = "POLITICS_PRIDI_PANOMYONG_REBEL_WIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/SIA/Portrait_Siam_Pridi_Panomyong_II.tga"
					expire = "1983.5.2"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { }
				}
				create_country_leader = { # Social Liberal
					name = "Thawan Thamrongnawasawat" # Thawan Thamrongnawasawat
					desc = "POLITICS_THAWAN_THAMRONGNAWASAWAT_DESC"

					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { }

				create_country_leader = { # Market Liberal
					name = "Pote Sarasin"
					desc = "POLITICS_POTE_SARASIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/SIA/Portrait_Siam_Pote_Sarasin.tga"

					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { }

				create_country_leader = { # Social Conservative
					name = "Kuekrit Pramoj"
					desc = "POLITICS_KUEKRIT_PRAMOJ_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/SIA/Portrait_Siam_Kuekrit_Pramoj.tga"

country_event = { #The fate of ceylon

	id = annex.119
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.119"}
	title = annex.119.t
	desc = annex.119.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

		trigger = {

			NOT = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}

		}

		name = annex.119.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = CEY
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			CEY = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = CEY

	}

	option = { #occupation

		trigger = {

			NOT = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}

		}

		name = annex.118.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05

		set_country_flag = CEY_CONQ

	}

	option = { #Integrate

		trigger = {

			OR = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}

		}

		name = annex.119.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}

		add_political_power = -20
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_war_support = -0.02

		add_state_core = 422

		set_country_flag = CEY_CONQ

	}

	option = { #puppet

		trigger = {

			OR = {
				tag = BHC
				tag = PRF
				tag = DEH
				original_tag = BHC
			}

		}

		name = annex.119.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}

		every_owned_state = {

			limit = {
				is_core_of = CEY
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			CEY = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = CEY

		remove_state_core = 422

	}
}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = SOM_CONQ

		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05

	}

	option = { #SOM

		name = annex.192.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 547
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {

				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOM
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				SOM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}

			}

			puppet = SOM

			else = {

				every_owned_state = {

					limit = {
						is_core_of = SOM
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_claimed_by = ROOT
							state = 892 #Failsafe for Jubaland
						}
					}

					SOM = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}

				}

				puppet = SOM

			}

		}

	}
}

	title = annex.210.t
	desc = annex.210.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LIB
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			"LIB" = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = LIB

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					"LIB" = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					}
				}
				"LIB" = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Deutscher Liberian Bund"
						name = "DLB"
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #liberate authdem (anybody but Germany and Mittelafrika)
		name = annex.210.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = LIB
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			"LIB" = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = LIB

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Authoritarian Dem."
						name = "Authoritarian Dem."
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.2.b

		}
		set_country_flag = LIB_CONQ

country_event = { #Cyprus Liberation
	id = annex.224
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.224"}
	title = annex.224.t
	desc = annex.224.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.224.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		CYP = {
			add_state_core = 183
			transfer_state = 183
		}

		puppet = CYP

	}

	option = { #Give it to the Turks
		name = annex.224.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				TUR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				is_in_faction_with = OTT
				OTT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}


		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = TUR
					TUR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
			TUR = { transfer_state = 183 }
			else = {
				OTT = { transfer_state = 183 }
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #Give it to Greece
		name = annex.224.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = GRE
				GRE = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		GRE = { transfer_state = 183 }

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.224.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.025
		add_war_support = -0.025
		set_country_flag = CYP_CONQ
	}

country_event = { #The destiny of North Italy for SIC
	id = annex.231
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.231"}
	title = annex.231.t
	desc = {
		text = annex.231.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = annex.231.d_confed
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SIC_confed
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.231.a #Italian Confederation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = SRD
				}
				SRD = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 160
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				VNC = {
					add_state_core = 160
					add_state_core = 759
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = VNC
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				VNC = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}

			puppet = VNC
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 159
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				LOM = {
					add_state_core = 159
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LOM
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				LOM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}

			puppet = LOM
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 1004
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				EMI = {
					add_state_core = 1004
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = EMI
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				EMI = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}

			puppet = EMI

		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 162
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				TUS = {
					add_state_core = 162
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUS
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				TUS = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}

			puppet = TUS
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 158
				country_exists = SRD
				NOT = { SRD = { is_subject = yes } }
			}
			SRD = { country_event = { id = annex.232 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 158
				NOT = { country_exists = SRD }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				SRD = {
					add_state_core = 158
					add_state_core = 1003
					add_state_core = 838
				}
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SRD
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				SRD = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}

			puppet = SRD
			SRD = { set_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = {
					NOT = {
						is_subject = yes
						AND = {
							is_in_faction = yes
							NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PAP
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				PAP = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}

			puppet = PAP

			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						PAP = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = PAP
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							NOT = {
								is_core_of = ROOT
								is_claimed_by = ROOT
							}
						}

						PAP = {
							transfer_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SIC_confed
	}

	option = { #Italian empire
		name = annex.231.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = SRD
				}
				SRD = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
		}
		set_country_flag = SIC_empire
		set_cosmetic_tag = SIC_ITA
		if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = SRD
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PAP = {
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						AND = {
							is_subject = no
							OR = {
								is_in_faction = no
								is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = PAP
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.231.c  #Give to SRD
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = SRD
			SRD = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					state = 1002
					state = 114
					state = 2

					state = 160
					state = 759
					is_core_of = SRD
				}
			}

			SRD = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

	}

country_event = { #Sardinia is asked if it wants to return to the mainland
	id = annex.232
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.232"}
	title = annex.232.t
	desc = annex.232.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.232.a #To Turin!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
			}
			CAN = { country_event = { id = annex.235 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = NFA
			}
			NFA = { country_event = { id = annex.235 } }
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}

		separate_peace_all_wars = yes

		FROM = { country_event = { id = annex.233 } }
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.232.b #No, we won't sell ourselves to a foreign power
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = annex.234 } }
	}
}

					JOR = { owns_state = 455 }
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = JOR
						JOR = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					IRQ = { owns_state = 455 }
					OR = {
						is_in_faction_with = IRQ
						IRQ = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		455 = {
			owner = {
				transfer_state = 453
				add_state_core = 453
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # transfer

		name = annex.237.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = EGY
				EGY = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

		}

country_event = { #The Fate of Honduras
	id = annex.252
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.252"}
	title = annex.252.t
	desc = annex.252.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #restore honduras
		name = annex.252.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = HON
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

			HON = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}

		}

		puppet = HON

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
					AND = {
						tag = NIC
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			HON = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = totalist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = totalist
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					AND = {
						NOT = {
							tag = NIC
						}
						has_government = social_democrat
					}
				}
			}
			HON = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
			HON = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.40
				}
			}
		}

	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.252.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = HON_CONQ
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.025
		add_war_support = -0.025
	}
}

country_event = { # The fate of an unified central america
	id = annex.255
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.255"}
	title = annex.255.t
	desc = annex.255.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
		}
	}

	option = { # Release a loyal unified central america
		name = annex.255.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CEN_conquered_release

		hidden_effect = {

			every_owned_state = {#Coring
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = GUA is_core_of = ELS is_core_of = HON is_core_of = NIC
						AND = {
							is_core_of = COS
							OR = {
								COS = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
								316 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
							}
						}
					}
				}

				add_core_of = CEN
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CEN
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}

				CEN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}

			}
			CEN = {
				ROOT = {
					puppet = CEN
				}
				transfer_state = 311
				transfer_state = 1071
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_socialist_government = yes }
					}
					load_focus_tree = Centroamerica_focus#Loads the Commie tree
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_elected_government = yes }
					}
					load_focus_tree = CA_DEM_focus
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_CON
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
						long_name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_REP
					load_focus_tree = CA_military_focus
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						HON = { exists = yes }
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = HON
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GUA = { exists = yes }
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = GUA
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NIC = { exists = yes }
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = NIC
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ELS = { exists = yes }
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = ELS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							COS = { exists = yes }
							OR = {
								COS = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
								owns_state = 316
							}
						}
					}
					COS = {
						every_owned_state = {
							add_core_of = CEN
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = COS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Release every nation seperately
		name = annex.255.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = release_cen_seperate
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = COS
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				COS = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = GUA
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				GUA = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = NIC
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				NIC = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = HON
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				HON = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ELS
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				ELS = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			GUA = {transfer_state = 311 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep it annexed
		name = annex.255.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = centroamerica_formed
					has_global_flag = demcen_formed
					has_global_flag = milcen_formed
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -150
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_war_support = -0.1
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {

				set_variable = { to_pay = 0}

				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag =  GUA_CONQ
							GUA = { exists = yes }
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { to_pay = 1}

				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag =  HON_CONQ
							HON = { exists = yes }
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { to_pay = 1}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag =  ELS_CONQ
							ELS = { exists = yes }
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { to_pay = 1}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag =  NIC_CONQ
							NIC = { exists = yes }
						}
					}
					add_to_variable = { to_pay = 1}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = COS_CONQ
								COS = { is_puppet_of = ROOT }
							}
							316 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
						}

					}
					add_to_variable = { to_pay = 1}

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						to_pay > 4
					}
				}
				add_political_power = -150
				add_stability = -0.15
				add_war_support = -0.15
				set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						to_pay > 3
					}
				}
				add_political_power = -120
				add_stability = -0.12
				add_war_support = -0.12
				set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						to_pay > 2
					}
				}
				add_political_power = -100
				add_stability = -0.10
				add_war_support = -0.10
				set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						to_pay > 0
					}
				}
				add_political_power = -50
				add_stability = -0.05
				add_war_support = -0.05
				set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			}
			else = { # Ought to never happen
				add_political_power = -10
			}
		}
	}

}



country_event = { # The giving of panama to central america
	id = annex.256
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.256"}
	title = annex.256.t
	desc = annex.256.d

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CEN_PAN_conq
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Give it all!
		name = annex.256.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PAN
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				add_core_of = CEN
			}
			CEN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep the canal
		name = annex.256.b
		trigger = {
			685 = {is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PAN
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					state = 685
				}

			}
			PREV = {
				add_core_of = CEN
			}
			CEN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep it annexed
		name = annex.256.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

}
